            // Polyfill for IE11
            Math.tanh = Math.tanh || function(x){
                var a = Math.exp(+x), b = Math.exp(-x);
                return a == Infinity ? 1 : (b == Infinity ? -1 : (a - b) / (a + b));
            }

            function degreesToRadians(deg) {
              return deg * (Math.PI / 180);
            }

            function radiansToDegrees(rad) {
              return rad / (Math.PI / 180);
            }

            function getBoundsAndZoomLevel(northLat, southLat, westLng, eastLng, spaceHeight, spaceWidth) {
                var WORLD_DIM = { height: 256, width: 256 };
                var ZOOM_MAX = 19;

                function latRad(lat) {
                    var sin = Math.sin(degreesToRadians(lat));
                    var radX2 = Math.log((1 + sin) / (1 - sin)) / 2;
                    return Math.max(Math.min(radX2, Math.PI), -Math.PI) / 2;
                }

                function fracToZoom(mapPx, worldPx, fraction) {
                    var v = Math.log(mapPx / worldPx / fraction) / Math.LN2;
                    // Adjust for floating error on exact fit
                    return Math.floor(v + 0.00001);
                }

                function zoomToFrac(mapPx, worldPx, zoom) {
                    return (mapPx / worldPx) / Math.exp(zoom * Math.LN2);
                }

                // ====================================================================
                // Calculate the zoom level to fit these bounds into the given viewport
                // ====================================================================

                // Sphere math to turn lat and long into degrees out of 360
                var latRadNorth = latRad(northLat);
                var latRadSouth = latRad(southLat);
                var latRadDiff = latRadNorth - latRadSouth;
                var latFraction = latRadDiff / Math.PI;

                var lngDiff = eastLng - westLng;
                var lngFraction = ((!(lngDiff >= 0)) ? (lngDiff + 360) : lngDiff) / 360;

                var latZoom = fracToZoom(spaceHeight, WORLD_DIM.height, latFraction);
                var lngZoom = fracToZoom(spaceWidth, WORLD_DIM.width, lngFraction);

                var finalZoom = Math.min(latZoom, lngZoom, ZOOM_MAX);

                // ========================================================
                // Calculate the viewport-exact bounds for this zoom level
                // ========================================================

                var fittedLngFraction = zoomToFrac(spaceWidth, WORLD_DIM.width, finalZoom);
                var lngDegreeCenter = (eastLng + westLng) / 2;
                var fittedLngDiff = lngDiff * (fittedLngFraction / lngFraction)
                var fittedWestLng = lngDegreeCenter - (fittedLngDiff / 2);
                var fittedEastLng = lngDegreeCenter + (fittedLngDiff / 2);

                var fittedLatRadFraction = zoomToFrac(spaceHeight, WORLD_DIM.height, finalZoom);
                var latRadCenter = (latRadNorth + latRadSouth) / 2;
                var fittedLatRadDiff = latRadDiff * (fittedLatRadFraction / latFraction);
                var fittedNorthLat = radiansToDegrees(Math.asin(Math.tanh(2 * (latRadCenter + (fittedLatRadDiff/2)))));
                var fittedSouthLat = radiansToDegrees(Math.asin(Math.tanh(2 * (latRadCenter - (fittedLatRadDiff/2)))));

                return {
                    zoom: finalZoom,
                    bounds: {
                        northLat: fittedNorthLat,
                        southLat: fittedSouthLat,
                        eastLng: fittedEastLng,
                        westLng: fittedWestLng,
                    }
                }
            }

            /*
                This must be kept synchronized with these vars in https://gitlab.zgtools.net/zillow/searchxp/static-search-page/-/blob/master/src/search-app/less/constants.less
                    @wideSingleColumnMinWidth
                    @wideDoubleColumnMinWidth
                    @searchListSingleColumnWidth_DoubleColTest
                    @searchListDoubleColumnWidth_DoubleColTest
            */
            function getListCardColumnWidth() {
                if (window.innerWidth >= 1280) {
                    return 750;
                } else if (window.innerWidth >= 1007) {
                    return 375;
                } else {
                    return 0;
                }
            }

            var northLat = 42.28575449532322;
            var southLat = 42.234936091389464;
            var westLng = -71.16694450378418;
            var eastLng = -71.0639476776123;

            var Z_HEADER_HEIGHT = 80;
            var SRP_HEADER_HEIGHT = 55;

            // Only prefetch when the window is wide enough to display a map and list view
            if (window.innerWidth >= 1007){
                var boundsAndZoom = getBoundsAndZoomLevel(northLat, southLat, westLng, eastLng, window.innerHeight - SRP_HEADER_HEIGHT - Z_HEADER_HEIGHT, window.innerWidth - getListCardColumnWidth());
                window.boundsAndZoom = boundsAndZoom;
                // Use a placeholder image one zoom level out, since we are stretching the image out 2x, which has the effect of zooming in.
                window.selectedPrefetch = window.mapPlaceholders[boundsAndZoom.zoom-1];

                // Kick off a prefetch since the image won't be actually consumed till SSP initial render
                document.querySelector("#mapPrefetch").href = window.selectedPrefetch;
            }
